import bpy

collection = bpy.data.collections.new("State")
bpy.context.scene.collection.children.link(collection)

cubeMesh = bpy.data.meshes.new("cube0")
color = bpy.data.materials.new("CubeColor")
color.diffuse_color = ( 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.9 )
cubeMesh.materials.append(color)
cubeObj = bpy.data.objects.new("cube0", cubeMesh)
cubeObj.location = bpy.context.scene.cursor.location
collection.objects.link(cubeObj)
cubeMesh.from_pydata([(-20, 18, -47), (27, 18, -47), (27, -36, -47), (-20, -36, -47), (-20, 18, 8), (27, 18, 8), (27, -36, 8), (-20, -36, 8)],[],[(0,1,2,3), (4,5,6,7), (0,4,5,1), (1,5,6,2), (2,6,7,3), (3,7,4,0)])
cubeMesh.update(calc_edges=True)

color.diffuse_color = ( 1.0, 2.4, 2.8, 0.9 )
cubeMesh.materials.append(color)
cubeObj = bpy.data.objects.new("cube19", cubeMesh)
cubeObj.location = bpy.context.scene.cursor.location
collection.objects.link(cubeObj)
cubeMesh.from_pydata([(-41, 44, -33), (10, 44, -33), (10, -7, -33), (-41, -7, -33), (-41, 44, 16), (10, 44, 16), (10, -7, 16), (-41, -7, 16)],[],[(0,1,2,3), (4,5,6,7), (0,4,5,1), (1,5,6,2), (2,6,7,3), (3,7,4,0)])
cubeMesh.update(calc_edges=True)
